ok {\n   217→\t\tobj = d.Obj\n   218→\t}\n   219→\tpod, ok := obj.(*v1.Pod)\n   220→\tif !ok {\n   221→\t\t// Not a pod?!\n   222→\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"enqueuePod called for unexpected object\", \"type\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%T\", obj))\n   223→\t\treturn\n   224→\t}\n   225→\n   226→\t// Check if pod has any resource claims to process.\n   227→\t// Extended resource claims are stored in pod.Status.ExtendedResourceClaimStatus,\n   228→\t// not in pod.Spec.ResourceClaims, so we need to check both locations.\n   229→\thasResourceClaims := len(pod.Spec.ResourceClaims) > 0\n   230→\t// For cleanup of extended resource claims, we must consider claims present\n   231→\t// in pod status regardless of the current feature gate state. The claim may\n   232→\t// have been created when the feature was enabled and still needs cleanup.\n   233→\thasExtendedResourceClaims := pod.Status.ExtendedResourceClaimStatus != nil\n   234→\tif !hasResourceClaims && !hasExtendedResourceClaims {\n   235→\t\t// Nothing to do for it at all.\n   236→\t\treturn\n   237→\t}\n   238→\n   239→\tif deleted {\n   240→\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"pod got deleted\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n   241→\t\tec.deletedObjects.Add(pod.UID)\n   242→\t}\n   243→\n   244→\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"pod with resource claims changed\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"deleted\", deleted)\n   245→\n   246→\t// Release reservations of a deleted or completed pod?\n   247→\tneedsClaims, reason := podNeedsClaims(pod, deleted)\n   248→\tif needsClaims {\n   249→\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"Not touching claims\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"reason\", reason)\n   250→\t} else {\n   251→\t\tfor _, podClaim := range pod.Spec.ResourceClaims {\n   252→\t\t\tclaimName, _, err := resourceclaim.Name(pod, &podClaim)\n   253→\t\t\tswitch {\n   254→\t\t\tcase err != nil:\n   255→\t\t\t\t// Either the claim was not created (nothing to do here) or\n   256→\t\t\t\t// the API changed. The later will also get reported elsewhere,\n   257→\t\t\t\t// so here it's just a debug message.\n   258→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"Nothing to do for claim during pod change\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name, \"err\", err, \"reason\", reason)\n   259→\t\t\tcase claimName != nil:\n   260→\t\t\t\tkey := claimKeyPrefix + pod.Namespace + \"/\" + *claimName\n   261→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"Process claim\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"claim\", klog.KRef(pod.Namespace, *claimName), \"key\", key, \"reason\", reason)\n   262→\t\t\t\tec.queue.Add(key)\n   263→\t\t\tdefault:\n   264→\t\t\t\t// Nothing to do, claim wasn't generated.\n   265→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"Nothing to do for skipped claim during pod change\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name, \"reason\", reason)\n   266→\t\t\t}\n   267→\t\t}\n   268→\n   269→\t\t// Process extended resource claims for completed/deleted pods.\n   270→\t\t// Extended resource pod.Status.ExtendedResourceClaimStatus.ResourceClaimName\n   276→\t\t\tkey := claimKeyPrefix + pod.Namespace + \"/\" + claimName\n   277→\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"Process extended resource claim\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"claim\", klog.KRef(pod.Namespace, claimName), \"key\", key, \"reason\", reason)\n   278→\t\t\tec.queue.Add(key)\n   279→\t\t}\n   280→\t}\n   281→\n   282→\tneedsWork, reason := ec.podNeedsWork(pod)\n   283→\tif needsWork {\n   284→\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"enqueing pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"reason\", reason)\n   285→\t\tec.queue.Add(podKeyPrefix + pod.Namespace + \"/\" + pod.Name)\n   286→\t\treturn\n   287→\t}\n   288→\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"not enqueing pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"reason\", reason)\n   289→}\n   290→\n   291→func podNeedsClaims(pod *v1.Pod, deleted bool) (bool, string) {\n   292→\tif deleted {\n   293→\t\treturn false, \"pod got removed\"\n   294→\t}\n   295→\tif podutil.IsPodTerminal(pod) {\n   296→\t\treturn false, \"pod has terminated\"\n   297→\t}\n   298→\tif pod.DeletionTimestamp != nil && pod.Spec.NodeName == \"\" {\n   299→\t\treturn false, \"pod got deleted before scheduling\"\n   300→\t}\n   301→\t// Still needs claims.\n   302→\treturn true, \"pod might run\"\n   303→}\n   304→\n   305→// podNeedsWork checks whether a new or modified pod needs to be processed\n   306→// further by a worker. It returns a boolean with the result and an explanation\n   307→// for it.\n   308→func (ec *Controller) podNeedsWork(pod *v1.Pod) (bool, string) {\n   309→\tif pod.DeletionTimestamp != nil {\n   310→\t\t// Nothing else to do for the pod.\n   311→\t\treturn false, \"pod is deleted\"\n   312→\t}\n   313→\n   314→\tfor _, podClaim := range pod.Spec.ResourceClaims {\n   315→\t\tclaimName, checkOwner, err := resourceclaim.Name(pod, &podClaim)\n   316→\t\tif err != nil {\n   317→\t\t\treturn true, err.Error()\n   318→\t\t}\n   319→\t\t// If the claimName is nil, then it has been determined before\n   320→\t\t// that the claim is not needed.\n   321→\t\tif claimName == nil {\n   322→\t\t\treturn false, \"claim is not needed\"\n   323→\t\t}\n   324→\t\tclaim, err := ec.claimLister.ResourceClaims(pod.Namespace).Get(*claimName)\n   325→\t\tif apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {\n   326→\t\t\tif podClaim.ResourceClaimTemplateName != nil {\n   327→\t\t\t\treturn true, \"must create ResourceClaim from template\"\n   328→\t\t\t}\n   329→\t\t\t// User needs to create claim.\n   330→\t\t\treturn false, \"claim is missing and must be created by user\"\n   331→\t\t}\n   332→\t\tif err != nil {\n   333→\t\t\t// Shouldn't happen.\n   334→\t\t\treturn true, fmt.Sprintf(\"internal error while checking for claim: %v\", err)\n   335→\t\t}\n   336→\n   337→\t\tif checkOwner {\n   338→\t\t\tif err := resourceclaim.IsForPod(pod, claim); err != nil {\n   339→\t\t\t\t// Cannot proceed with the pod unless that other claim gets deleted.\n   340→\t\t\t\treturn false, err.Error()\n   341→\t\t\t}\n   342→\t\t}\n   343→\n   344→\t\t// This check skips over the reasons below that only apply\n   345→\t\t// when a pod has been scheduled already. We need to keep checking\n   346→\t\t// for more claims that might need to be created.\n   347→\t\tif pod.Spec.NodeName == \"\" {\n   348→\t\t\tcontinue\n   349→\t\t}\n   350→\n   351→\t\tif claim.Status.Allocation != nil &&\n   352→\t\t\t!resourceclaim.IsReservedForPod(pod, claim) &&\n   353→\t\t\tresourceclaim.CanBeReserved(claim) {\n   354→\t\t\t// Need to reserve it.\n   355→\t\t\treturn true, fmt.Sprintf(\"need to reserve claim %s for pod\", klog.KObj(claim))\n   356→\t\t}\n   357→\t}\n   358→\n   359→\treturn false, \"nothing to do\"\n   360→}\n   361→\n   362→func (ec *Controller) enqueueResourceClaim(logger klog.Logger, oldObj, newObj interface{}) {\n   363→\tdeleted := newObj == nil\n   364→\tif d, ok := oldObj.(cache.DeletedFinalStateUnknown); ok {\n   365→\t\toldObj = d.Obj\n   366→\t}\n   367→\toldClaim, ok := oldObj.(*resourceapi.ResourceClaim)\n   368→\tif oldObj != nil && !ok {\n   369→\t\treturn\n   370→\t}\n   371→\tnewClaim, ok := newObj.(*resourceapi.ResourceClaim)\n   372→\tif newObj != nil && !ok {\n   373→\t\treturn\n   374→\t}\n   375→\n   376→\t// Check if both the old and new claim are nil in case DeletedFinalStateUnknown.Obj can be nil.\n   377→\tif oldClaim == nil && newClaim == nil {\n   378→\t\treturn\n   379→\t}\n   380→\n   381→\tclaim := newClaim\n   382→\tif claim == nil {\n   383→\t\tclaim = oldClaim\n   384→\t}\n   385→\tif !deleted {\n   386→\t\t// When starting up, we have to check all claims to find those with\n   387→\t\t// stale pods in ReservedFor. During an update, a pod might get added\n   388→\t\t// that already no longer exists.\n   389→\t\tkey := claimKeyPrefix + claim.Namespace + \"/\" + claim.Name\n   390→\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"enqueing new or updated claim\", \"claim\", klog.KObj(claim), \"key\", key)\n   391→\t\tec.queue.Add(key)\n   392→\t} else {\n   393→\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"not enqueing deleted claim\", \"claim\", klog.KObj(claim))\n   394→\t}\n   395→\n   396→\t// Also check whether this causes work for any of the currently\n   397→\t// known pods which use the ResourceClaim.\n   398→\tobjs, err := ec.podIndexer.ByIndex(podResourceClaimIndex, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s/%s\", claim.Namespace, claim.Name))\n   399→\tif err != nil {\n   400→\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"listing pods from cache\")\n   401→\t\treturn\n   402→\t}\n   403→\tif len(objs) == 0 {\n   404→\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"unrelated to any known pod\", \"claim\", klog.KObj(claim))\n   405→\t\treturn\n   406→\t}\n   407→\tfor _, obj := range objs {\n   408→\t\tec.enqueuePod(logger, obj, false)\n   409→\t}\n   410→}\n   411→\n   412→func (ec *Controller) Run(ctx context.Context, workers int) {\n   413→\tdefer runtime.HandleCrashWithContext(ctx)\n   414→\tdefer ec.queue.ShutDown()\n   415→\n   416→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   417→\tlogger.Info(\"Starting resource claim controller\")\n   418→\tdefer logger.Info(\"Shutting down resource claim controller\")\n   419→\n   420→\teventBroadcaster := record.NewBroadcaster(record.WithContext(ctx))\n   421→\teventBroadcaster.StartLogging(klog.Infof)\n   422→\teventBroadcaster.StartRecordingToSink(&v1core.EventSinkImpl{Interface: ec.kubeClient.CoreV1().Events(\"\")})\n   423→\tec.recorder = eventBroadcaster.NewRecorder(scheme.Scheme, v1.EventSource{Component: \"resource_claim\"})\n   424→\tdefer eventBroadcaster.Shutdown()\n   425→\n   426→\tif !cache.WaitForNamedCacheSyncWithContext(ctx, ec.podSynced, ec.claimsSynced, ec.templatesSynced) {\n   427→\t\treturn\n   428→\t}\n   429→\n   430→\tfor i := 0; i < workers; i++ {\n   431→\t\tgo wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, ec.runWorker, time.Second)\n   432→\t}\n   433→\n   434→\t<-ctx.Done()\n   435→}\n   436→\n   437→func (ec *Controller) runWorker(ctx context.Context) {\n   438→\tfor ec.processNextWorkItem(ctx) {\n   439→\t}\n   440→}\n   441→\n   442→func (ec *Controller) processNextWorkItem(ctx context.Context) bool {\n   443→\tkey, shutdown := ec.queue.Get()\n   444→\tif shutdown {\n   445→\t\treturn false\n   446→\t}\n   447→\tdefer ec.queue.Done(key)\n   448→\n   449→\terr := ec.syncHandler(ctx, key)\n   450→\tif err == nil {\n   451→\t\tec.queue.Forget(key)\n   452→\t\treturn true\n   453→\t}\n   454→\n   455→\truntime.HandleErrorWithContext(ctx, err, \"Work item failed\", \"item\", key)\n   456→\tec.queue.AddRateLimited(key)\n   457→\n   458→\treturn true\n   459→}\n   460→\n   461→// syncHandler is invoked for each work item which might need to be processed.\n   462→// If an error is returned from this function, the item will be requeued.\n   463→func (ec *Controller) syncHandler(ctx context.Context, key string) error {\n   464→\tsep := strings.Index(key, \":\")\n   465→\tif sep < 0 {\n   466→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected key: %s\", key)\n   467→\t}\n   468→\tprefix, object := key[0:sep+1], key[sep+1:]\n   469→\tnamespace, name, err := cache.SplitMetaNamespaceKey(object)\n   470→\tif err != nil {\n   471→\t\treturn err\n   472→\t}\n   473→\n   474→\tswitch prefix {\n   475→\tcase podKeyPrefix:\n   476→\t\treturn ec.syncPod(ctx, namespace, name)\n   477→\tcase claimKeyPrefix:\n   478→\t\treturn ec.syncClaim(ctx, namespace, name)\n   479→\tdefault:\n   480→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected key prefix: %s\", prefix)\n   481→\t}\n   482→\n   483→}\n   484→\n   485→func (ec *Controller) syncPod(ctx context.Context, namespace, name string) error {\n   486→\tlogger := klog.LoggerWithValues(klog.FromContext(ctx), \"pod\", klog.KRef(namespace, name))\n   487→\tctx = klog.NewContext(ctx, logger)\n   488→\tpod, err := ec.podLister.Pods(namespace).Get(name)\n   489→\tif err != nil {\n   490→\t\tif apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {\n   491→\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"nothing to do for pod, it is gone\")\n   492→\t\t\treturn nil\n   493→\t\t}\n   494→\t\treturn err\n   495→\t}\n   496→\n   497→\t// Ignore pods which are already getting deleted.\n   498→\tif pod.DeletionTimestamp != nil {\n   499→\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"nothing to do for pod, it is marked for deletion\")\n   500→\t\treturn nil\n   501→\t}\n   502→\n   503→\tvar newPodClaims map[string]string\n   504→\tfor _, podClaim := range pod.Spec.ResourceClaims {\n   505→\t\tif err := ec.handleClaim(ctx, pod, podClaim, &newPodClaims); err != nil {\n   506→\t\t\tif ec.recorder != nil {\n   507→\t\t\t\tec.recorder.Event(pod, v1.EventTypeWarning, \"FailedResourceClaimCreation\", fmt.Sprintf(\"PodResourceClaim %s: %v\", podClaim.Name, err))\n   508→\t\t\t}\n   509→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"pod %s/%s, PodResourceClaim %s: %v\", namespace, name, podClaim.Name, err)\n   510→\t\t}\n   511→\t}\n   512→\n   513→\tif newPodClaims != nil {\n   514→\t\t// Patch the pod status with the new information about\n   515→\t\t// generated ResourceClaims.\n   516→\t\tstatuses := make([]*corev1apply.PodResourceClaimStatusApplyConfiguration, 0, len(newPodClaims))\n   517→\t\tfor podClaimName, resourceClaimName := range newPodClaims {\n   518→\t\t\tstatuses = append(statuses, corev1apply.PodResourceClaimStatus().WithName(podClaimName).WithResourceClaimName(resourceClaimName))\n   519→\t\t}\n   520→\t\tpodApply := corev1apply.Pod(name, namespace).WithStatus(corev1apply.PodStatus().WithResourceClaimStatuses(statuses...))\n   521→\t\tif _, err := ec.kubeClient.CoreV1().Pods(namespace).ApplyStatus(ctx, podApply, metav1.ApplyOptions{FieldManager: fieldManager, Force: true}); err != nil {\n   522→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"update pod %s/%s ResourceClaimStatuses: %v\", namespace, name, err)\n   523→\t\t}\n   524→\t}\n   525→\n   526→\tif pod.Spec.NodeName == \"\" {\n   527→\t\t// Scheduler will handle reservations.\n   528→\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"nothing to do for pod, scheduler will deal with it\")\n   529→\t\treturn nil\n   530→\t}\n   531→\n   532→\tfor _, podClaim := range pod.Spec.ResourceClaims {\n   533→\t\tclaimName, checkOwner, err := resourceclaim.Name(pod, &podClaim)\n   534→\t\tif err != nil {\n   535→\t\t\treturn err\n   536→\t\t}\n   537→\t\t// If nil, then it has been determined that the claim is not needed\n   538→\t\t// and can be skipped.\n   539→\t\tif claimName == nil {\n   540→\t\t\tcontinue\n   541→\t\t}\n   542→\t\tclaim, err := ec.claimLister.ResourceClaims(pod.Namespace).Get(*claimName)\n   543→\t\tif err != nil {\n   544→\t\t\tif apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {\n   545→\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   546→\t\t\t}\n   547→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"retrieve claim: %v\", err)\n   548→\t\t}\n   549→\t\tif checkOwner {\n   550→\t\t\tif err := resourceclaim.IsForPod(pod, claim); err != nil {\n   551→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   552→\t\t\t}\n   553→\t\t}\n   554→\t\tif claim.Status.Allocation != nil &&\n   555→\t\t\t!resourceclaim.IsReservedForPod(pod, claim) &&\n   556→\t\t\tresourceclaim.CanBeReserved(claim) {\n   557→\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"reserve claim for pod\", \"resourceClaim\", klog.KObj(claim))\n   558→\t\t\tif err := ec.reserveForPod(ctx, pod, claim); err != nil {\n   559→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   560→\t\t\t}\n   561→\t\t}\n   562→\t}\n   563→\n   564→\treturn nil\n   565→}\n   566→\n   567→// handleClaim is invoked for each resource claim of a pod.\n   568→func (ec *Controller) handleClaim(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod, podClaim v1.PodResourceClaim, newPodClaims *map[string]string) error {\n   569→\tlogger := klog.LoggerWithValues(klog.FromContext(ctx), \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name)\n   570→\tctx = klog.NewContext(ctx, logger)\n   571→\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"checking\", \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name)\n   572→\n   573→\t// resourceclaim.Name checks for the situation that the client doesn't\n   574→\t// know some future addition to the API. Therefore it gets called here\n   575→\t// even if there is no template to work on, because if some new field\n   576→\t// gets added, the expectation might be that the controller does\n   577→\t// something for it.\n   578→\tclaimName, mustCheckOwner, err := resourceclaim.Name(pod, &podClaim)\n   579→\tswitch {\n   580→\tcase errors.Is(err, resourceclaim.ErrClaimNotFound):\n   581→\t\t// Continue below.\n   582→\tcase err != nil:\n   583→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"checking for claim before creating it: %v\", err)\n   584→\tcase claimName == nil:\n   585→\t\t// Nothing to do, no claim needed.\n   586→\t\treturn nil\n   587→\tcase *claimName != \"\":\n   588→\t\tclaimName := *claimName\n   589→\t\t// The ResourceClaim should exist because it is recorded in the pod.status.resourceClaimStatuses,\n   590→\t\t// but perhaps it was deleted accidentally. In that case we re-create it.\n   591→\t\tclaim, err := ec.claimLister.ResourceClaims(pod.Namespace).Get(claimName)\n   592→\t\tif err != nil && !apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {\n   593→\t\t\treturn err\n   594→\t\t}\n   595→\t\tif claim != nil {\n   596→\t\t\tvar err error\n   597→\t\t\tif mustCheckOwner {\n   598→\t\t\t\terr = resourceclaim.IsForPod(pod, claim)\n   599→\t\t\t}\n   600→\t\t\tif err == nil {\n   601→\t\t\t\t// Already created, nothing more to do.\n   602→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"claim already created\", \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name, \"resourceClaim\", claimName)\n   603→\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   604→\t\t\t}\n   605→\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"claim that was created for the pod is no longer owned by the pod, creating a new one\", \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name, \"resourceClaim\", claimName)\n   606→\t\t}\n   607→\t}\n   608→\n   609→\ttemplateName := podClaim.ResourceClaimTemplateName\n   610→\tif templateName == nil {\n   611→\t\t// Nothing to do.\n   612→\t\treturn nil\n   613→\t}\n   614→\n   615→\t// Before we create a new ResourceClaim, check if there is an orphaned one.\n   616→\t// This covers the case that the controller has created it, but then fails\n   617→\t// before it can update the pod status.\n   618→\tclaim, err := ec.findPodResourceClaim(pod, podClaim)\n   619→\tif err != nil {\n   620→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"finding ResourceClaim for claim %s in pod %s/%s failed: %v\", podClaim.Name, pod.Namespace, pod.Name, err)\n   621→\t}\n   622→\n   623→\tif claim == nil {\n   624→\t\ttemplate, err := ec.templateLister.ResourceClaimTemplates(pod.Namespace).Get(*templateName)\n   625→\t\tif err != nil {\n   626→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"resource claim template %q: %v\", *templateName, err)\n   627→\t\t}\n   628→\n   629→\t\tif !ec.features.AdminAccess && needsAdminAccess(template) {\n   630→\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"admin access is requested, but the feature is disabled\")\n   631→\t\t}\n   632→\n   633→\t\tif !ec.features.PrioritizedList && hasPrioritizedList(template) {\n   634→\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"template includes a prioritized list of subrequests, but the feature is disabled\")\n   635→\t\t}\n   636→\n   637→\t\t// Create the ResourceClaim with pod as owner, with a generated name that uses\n   638→\t\t// <pod>-<claim name> as base.\n   639→\t\tisTrue := true\n   640→\t\tannotations := template.Spec.ObjectMeta.Annotations\n   641→\t\tif annotations == nil {\n   642→\t\t\tannotations = make(map[string]string)\n   643→\t\t}\n   644→\t\tannotations[podResourceClaimAnnotation] = podClaim.Name\n   645→\t\tgenerateName := pod.Name + \"-\" + podClaim.Name + \"-\"\n   646→\t\tmaxBaseLen := 57 // Leave space for hyphen and 5 random characters in a name with 63 characters.\n   647→\t\tif len(generateName) > maxBaseLen {\n   648→\t\t\t// We could leave truncation to the apiserver, but as\n   649→\t\t\t// it removes at the end, we would loose everything\n   650→\t\t\t// from the pod claim name when the pod name is long.\n   651→\t\t\t// We can do better and truncate both strings,\n   652→\t\t\t// proportional to their length.\n   653→\t\t\tgenerateName = pod.Name[0:len(pod.Name)*maxBaseLen/len(generateName)] +\n   654→\t\t\t\t\"-\" +\n   655→\t\t\t\tpodClaim.Name[0:len(podClaim.Name)*maxBaseLen/len(generateName)]\n   656→\t\t}\n   657→\t\tclaim = &resourceapi.ResourceClaim{\n   658→\t\t\tObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{\n   659→\t\t\t\tGenerateName: generateName,\n   660→\t\t\t\tOwnerReferences: []metav1.OwnerReference{\n   661→\t\t\t\t\t{\n   662→\t\t\t\t\t\tAPIVersion: \"v1\",\n   663→\t\t\t\t\t\tKind:       \"Pod\",\n   664→\t\t\t\t\t\tName:       pod.Name,\n   665→\t\t\t\t\t\tUID:        pod.UID,\n   666→\t\t\t\t\t\tController: &isTrue,\n   667→\t\t\t\t\t},\n   668→\t\t\t\t},\n   669→\t\t\t\tAnnotations: annotations,\n   670→\t\t\t\tLabels:      template.Spec.ObjectMeta.Labels,\n   671→\t\t\t},\n   672→\t\t\tSpec: template.Spec.Spec,\n   673→\t\t}\n   674→\t\tmetricLabel := getAdminAccessMetricLabel(claim)\n   675→\t\tclaimName := claim.Name\n   676→\t\tclaim, err = ec.kubeClient.ResourceV1().ResourceClaims(pod.Namespace).Create(ctx, claim, metav1.CreateOptions{})\n   677→\t\tif err != nil {\n   678→\t\t\tresourceclaimmetrics.ResourceClaimCreate.WithLabelValues(\"failure\", metricLabel).Inc()\n   679→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create ResourceClaim %s: %v\", claimName, err)\n   680→\t\t}\n   681→\t\tresourceclaimmetrics.ResourceClaimCreate.WithLabelValues(\"success\", metricLabel).Inc()\n   682→\t\tlogger.V(4).Info(\"Created ResourceClaim\", \"claim\", klog.KObj(claim), \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n   683→\t\tec.claimCache.Mutation(claim)\n   684→\t}\n   685→\n   686→\t// Remember the new ResourceClaim for a batch PodStatus update in our caller.\n   687→\tif *newPodClaims == nil {\n   688→\t\t*newPodClaims = make(map[string]string)\n   689→\t}\n   690→\t(*newPodClaims)[podClaim.Name] = claim.Name\n   691→\n   692→\treturn nil\n   693→}\n   694→\n   695→func needsAdminAccess(claimTemplate *resourceapi.ResourceClaimTemplate) bool {\n   696→\tfor _, request := range claimTemplate.Spec.Spec.Devices.Requests {\n   697→\t\tif request.Exactly != nil && ptr.Deref(request.Exactly.AdminAccess, false) {\n   698→\t\t\treturn true\n   699→\t\t}\n   700→\t}\n   701→\treturn false\n   702→}\n   703→\n   704→func hasPrioritizedList(claimTemplate *resourceapi.ResourceClaimTemplate) bool {\n   705→\tfor _, request := range claimTemplate.Spec.Spec.Devices.Requests {\n   706→\t\tif len(request.FirstAvailable) > 0 {\n   707→\t\t\treturn true\n   708→\t\t}\n   709→\t}\n   710→\treturn false\n   711→}\n   712→\n   713→// findPodResourceClaim looks for an existing ResourceClaim with the right\n   714→// annotation (ties it to the pod claim) and the right ownership (ties it to\n   715→// the pod).\n   716→func (ec *Controller) findPodResourceClaim(pod *v1.Pod, podClaim v1.PodResourceClaim) (*resourceapi.ResourceClaim, error) {\n   717→\t// Only claims owned by the pod will get returned here.\n   718→\tclaims, err := ec.claimCache.ByIndex(claimPodOwnerIndex, string(pod.UID))\n   719→\tif err != nil {\n   720→\t\treturn nil, err\n   721→\t}\n   722→\tfor _, claimObj := range claims {\n   723→\t\tclaim, ok := claimObj.(*resourceapi.ResourceClaim)\n   724→\t\tif !ok {\n   725→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected object of type %T returned by claim cache\", claimObj)\n   726→\t\t}\n   727→\t\tpodClaimName, ok := claim.Annotations[podResourceClaimAnnotation]\n   728→\t\t// No annotation? Then it cannot be an automatically generated claim\n   729→\t\t// and we need to ignore it.\n   730→\t\tif !ok {\n   731→\t\t\tcontinue\n   732→\t\t}\n   733→\n   734→\t\t// Not the claim for this particular pod claim?\n   735→\t\tif podClaimName != podClaim.Name {\n   736→\t\t\tcontinue\n   737→\t\t}\n   738→\n   739→\t\t// Pick the first one that matches. There shouldn't be more than one. If there is,\n   740→\t\t// then all others will be ignored until the pod gets deleted. Then they also get\n   741→\t\t// cleaned up.\n   742→\t\treturn claim, nil\n   743→\t}\n   744→\treturn nil, nil\n   745→}\n   746→\n   747→func (ec *Controller) reserveForPod(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod, claim *resourceapi.ResourceClaim) error {\n   748→\tclaim = claim.DeepCopy()\n   749→\tclaim.Status.ReservedFor = append(claim.Status.ReservedFor,\n   750→\t\tresourceapi.ResourceClaimConsumerReference{\n   751→\t\t\tResource: \"pods\",\n   752→\t\t\tName:     pod.Name,\n   753→\t\t\tUID:      pod.UID,\n   754→\t\t})\n   755→\tif _, err := ec.kubeClient.ResourceV1().ResourceClaims(claim.Namespace).UpdateStatus(ctx, claim, metav1.UpdateOptions{}); err != nil {\n   756→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"reserve claim %s for pod: %w\", klog.KObj(claim), err)\n   757→\t}\n   758→\treturn nil\n   759→}\n   760→\n   761→func (ec *Controller) syncClaim(ctx context.Context, namespace, name string) error {\n   762→\tlogger := klog.LoggerWithValues(klog.FromContext(ctx), \"claim\", klog.KRef(namespace, name))\n   763→\tctx = klog.NewContext(ctx, logger)\n   764→\tclaim, err := ec.claimLister.ResourceClaims(namespace).Get(name)\n   765→\tif err != nil {\n   766→\t\tif apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {\n   767→\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"nothing to do for claim, it is gone\")\n   768→\t\t\treturn nil\n   769→\t\t}\n   770→\t\treturn err\n   771→\t}\n   772→\n   773→\t// Check if the ReservedFor entries are all still valid.\n   774→\tvalid := make([]resourceapi.ResourceClaimConsumerReference, 0, len(claim.Status.ReservedFor))\n   775→\tfor _, reservedFor := range claim.Status.ReservedFor {\n   776→\t\tif reservedFor.APIGroup == \"\" &&\n   777→\t\t\treservedFor.Resource == \"pods\" {\n   778→\t\t\t// A pod falls into one of three categories:\n   779→\t\t\t// - we have it in our cache -> don't remove it until we are told that it got removed\n   780→\t\t\t// - we don't have it in our cache anymore, but we have seen it before -> it was deleted, remove it\n   781→\t\t\t// - not in our cache, not seen -> double-check with API server before removal\n   782→\n   783→\t\t\tkeepEntry := true\n   784→\n   785→\t\t\t// Tracking deleted pods in the LRU cache is an\n   786→\t\t\t// optimization. Without this cache, the code would\n   787→\t\t\t// have to do the API call below for every deleted pod\n   788→\t\t\t// to ensure that the pod really doesn't exist. With\n   789→\t\t\t// the cache, most of the time the pod will be recorded\n   790→\t\t\t// as deleted and the API call can be avoided.\n   791→\t\t\tif ec.deletedObjects.Has(reservedFor.UID) {\n   792→\t\t\t\t// We know that the pod was deleted. We have to be\n   804→\t\t\t\t\t// absolutely sure and thus have to check with\n   805→\t\t\t\t\t// the API server.\n   806→\t\t\t\t\tpod, err := ec.kubeClient.CoreV1().Pods(claim.Namespace).Get(ctx, reservedFor.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})\n   807→\t\t\t\t\tif err != nil && !apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {\n   808→\t\t\t\t\t\treturn err\n   809→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   810→\t\t\t\t\tif pod == nil || pod.UID != reservedFor.UID {\n   811→\t\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"remove reservation because pod is gone or got replaced\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"claim\", klog.KRef(namespace, name))\n   812→\t\t\t\t\t\tkeepEntry = false\n   813→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   814→\t\t\t\tcase pod.UID != reservedFor.UID:\n   815→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"remove reservation because pod got replaced with new instance\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"claim\", klog.KRef(namespace, name))\n   816→\t\t\t\t\tkeepEntry = false\n   817→\t\t\t\tcase isPodDone(pod):\n   818→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"remove reservation because pod will not run anymore\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"claim\", klog.KRef(namespace, name))\n   819→\t\t\t\t\tkeepEntry = false\n   820→\t\t\t\t}\n   821→\t\t\t}\n   822→\n 830→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unsupported ReservedFor entry: %v\", reservedFor)\n   831→\t}\n   832→\n   833→\tbuiltinControllerFinalizer := slices.Index(claim.Finalizers, resourceapi.Finalizer)\n   834→\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"claim reserved for counts\", \"currentCount\", len(claim.Status.ReservedFor), \"claim\", klog.KRef(namespace, name), \"updatedCount\", len(valid), \"builtinController\", builtinControllerFinalizer >= 0)\n   835→\tif len(valid) < len(claim.Status.ReservedFor) {\n   836→\t\t// This is not using a patch because we want the update to fail if anything\n   837→\t\t// changed in the meantime.\n   838→\t\tclaim := claim.DeepCopy()\n   839→\t\tclaim.Status.ReservedFor = valid\n   840→\n   841→\t\t// DRA always performs delayed allocations. Relatedly, it also\n   842→\t\t// deallocates a claim as soon as the last consumer stops using\n   843→\t\t// it. This ensures that the claim can be allocated again as needed by\n   844→\t\t// some future consumer instead of trying to schedule that consumer\n   845→\t\t// onto the node that was chosen for the previous consumer. It also\n   846→\t\t// releases the underlying resources for use by other claims.\n   847→\t\t//\n   848→\t\t// This has to be triggered by the transition from \"was being used\" to\n   849→\t\t// \"is not used anymore\" because a DRA driver is not required to set\n   850→\t\t// `status.reservedFor` together with `status.allocation`, i.e. a claim\n   851→\t\t// that is \"currently unused\" should not get deallocated.\n   852→\t\t//\n   853→\t\t// This does not matter for claims that were created for a pod. err)\n   124→\t}\n   125→\n   126→\thealthInfoCache, err := newHealthInfoCache(filepath.Join(stateFileDirectory, \"dra_health_state\"))\n   127→\tif err != nil {\n   128→\t\treturn nil, configurable in the future.\n   133→\treconcilePeriod := defaultReconcilePeriod\n   134→\n   135→\tmanager := &Manager{\n   136→\t\tcache:           claimInfoCache,\n   137→\t\tkubeClient:      kubeClient,\n   138→\t\treconcilePeriod: reconcilePeriod,\n   139→\t\tactivePods:      nil,\n   140→\t\tsourcesReady:    nil,\n   141→\t\thealthInfoCache: healthInfoCache,\n   142→\t\tupdate:          make(chan resourceupdates.Update, 100),\n   143→\t}\n   144→\n   145→\treturn manager, nil\n   146→}\n   147→\n   148→func (m *Manager) NewMetricsCollector() metrics.StableCollector {\n   149→\treturn &claimInfoCollector{cache: m.cache}\n   150→}\n   151→\n   152→// GetWatcherHandler must be called after Start, it indirectly depends\n   153→// on parameters which only get passed to Start, for example the context.\n   154→func (m *Manager) GetWatcherHandler() cache.PluginHandler {\n   155→\treturn m.draPlugins\n   156→}\n   157→\n   158→// Start starts the reconcile loop of the manager.\n   159→func (m *Manager) Start(ctx context.Context, activePods ActivePodsFunc, getNode GetNodeFunc, sourcesReady config.SourcesReady) error {\n   160→\tm.initDRAPluginManager(ctx, getNode, defaultWipingDelay)\n   161→\tm.activePods = activePods\n   162→\tm.sourcesReady = sourcesReady\n   163→\tgo wait.UntilWithContext(ctx, func(ctx context.Context) { m.reconcileLoop(ctx) }, m.reconcilePeriod)\n   164→\treturn nil\n   165→}\n   166→\n   167→// initPluginManager can be used instead of Start to make the manager useable\n   168→// for calls to prepare/unprepare. It exists primarily for testing purposes.\n   169→func (m *Manager) initDRAPluginManager(ctx context.Context, getNode GetNodeFunc, wipingDelay time.Duration) {\n   170→\tm.draPlugins = draplugin.NewDRAPluginManager(ctx, m.kubeClient, getNode, m, wipingDelay)\n   171→}\n   172→\n   173→// reconcileLoop ensures that any stale state in the manager's claimInfoCache gets periodically reconciled.\n   174→func (m *Manager) reconcileLoop(ctx context.Context) {\n   175→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   176→\t// Only once all sources are ready do we attempt to reconcile.\n   177→\t// This ensures that the call to m.activePods() below will succeed with\n   178→\t// the actual active pods list.\n   179→\tif m.sourcesReady == nil || !m.sourcesReady.AllReady() {\n   180→\t\treturn\n   181→\t}\n   182→\n   183→\t// Get the full list of active pods.\n   184→\tactivePods := sets.New[string]()\n   185→\tfor _, p := range m.activePods() {\n   186→\t\tactivePods.Insert(string(p.UID))\n   187→\t}\n   188→\n   189→\t// Get the list of inactive pods still referenced by any claimInfos.\n   190→\ttype podClaims struct {\n   191→\t\tuid        types.UID\n   192→\t\tnamespace  string\n   193→\t\tclaimNames []string\n   194→\t}\n   195→\tinactivePodClaims := make(map[string]*podClaims)\n   196→\tm.cache.RLock()\n   197→\tfor _, claimInfo := range m.cache.claimInfo {\n   198→\t\tfor podUID := range claimInfo.PodUIDs {\n   199→\t\t\tif activePods.Has(podUID) {\n   200→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   201→\t\t\t}\n   202→\t\t\tif inactivePodClaims[podUID] == nil {\n   203→\t\t\t\tinactivePodClaims[podUID] = &podClaims{\n   204→\t\t\t\t\tuid:        types.UID(podUID),\n   205→\t\t\t\t\tnamespace:  claimInfo.Namespace,\n   206→\t\t\t\t\tclaimNames: []string{},\n   207→\t\t\t\t}\n   208→\t\t\t}\n   209→\t\t\tinactivePodClaims[podUID].claimNames = append(inactivePodClaims[podUID].claimNames, claimInfo.ClaimName)\n   210→\t\t}\n   211→\t}\n   212→\tm.cache.RUnlock()\n   213→\n   214→\t// Loop through all inactive pods and call UnprepareResources on them.\n   215→\tfor _, podClaims := range inactivePodClaims {\n   216→\t\tif err := m.unprepareResources(ctx, podClaims.uid, podClaims.namespace, podClaims.claimNames); err != nil {\n   217→\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Unpreparing pod resources in reconcile loop failed, will retry\", \"podUID\", podClaims.uid, \"err\", err)\n   218→\t\t}\n   219→\t}\n   220→}\n   221→\n   222→// PrepareResources attempts to prepare all of the required resources\n   223→// for the input container, issue NodePrepareResources rpc requests\n   224→// for each new resource requirement, process their responses and update the cached\n   225→// containerResources on success.\n   226→func (m *Manager) PrepareResources(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod) error {\n   227→\tstartTime := time.Now()\n   228→\terr := m.prepareResources(ctx, pod)\n   229→\tkubeletmetrics.DRAOperationsDuration.WithLabelValues(\"PrepareResources\", strconv.FormatBool(err == nil)).Observe(time.Since(startTime).Seconds())\n   230→\tif err != nil {\n   231→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"prepare dynamic resources: %w\", err)\n   232→\t}\n   233→\treturn nil\n   234→}\n   235→\n   236→func (m *Manager) prepareResources(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod) error {\n   237→\tvar err error\n   238→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   239→\tbatches := make(map[*draplugin.DRAPlugin][]*drapb.Claim)\n   240→\tresourceClaims := make(map[types.UID]*resourceapi.ResourceClaim)\n   241→\n   242→\t// Do a validation pass *without* changing the claim info cache.\n   243→\t// If anything goes wrong, we don't proceed. This has the advantage\n   244→\t// that the failing pod can be deleted without getting stuck.\n   245→\t//\n   246→\t// If we added the claim and pod to the cache, UnprepareResources\n   247→\t// would have to asssume that NodePrepareResources was called and\n   248→\t// try to call NodeUnprepareResources. This is particularly bad\n   249→\t// when the driver never has been installed on the node and\n   250→\t// remains unavailable.\n   251→\tpodResourceClaims := pod.Spec.ResourceClaims\n   252→\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(kubefeatures.DRAExtendedResource) {\n   253→\t\tif pod.Status.ExtendedResourceClaimStatus != nil {\n   254→\t\t\textendedResourceClaim := v1.PodResourceClaim{\n   255→\t\t\t\tResourceClaimName: &pod.Status.ExtendedResourceClaimStatus.ResourceClaimName,\n   256→\t\t\t}\n   257→\t\t\tpodResourceClaims = make([]v1.PodResourceClaim, 0, len(pod.Spec.ResourceClaims)+1)\n   258→\t\t\tpodResourceClaims = append(podResourceClaims, pod.Spec.ResourceClaims...)\n   259→\t\t\tpodResourceClaims = append(podResourceClaims, extendedResourceClaim)\n   260→\t\t}\n   261→\t}\n   262→\tinfos := make([]struct {\n   263→\t\tresourceClaim *resourceapi.ResourceClaim\n   264→\t\tpodClaim      *v1.PodResourceClaim\n   265→\t\tclaimInfo     *ClaimInfo\n   266→\t\tplugins       map[string]*draplugin.DRAPlugin\n   267→\t}, len(podResourceClaims))\n   268→\tfor i := range podResourceClaims {\n   269→\t\tpodClaim := &podResourceClaims[i]\n   270→\t\tinfos[i].podClaim = podClaim\n   271→\t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Processing resource\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name)\n   272→\t\tclaimName, mustCheckOwner, err := resourceclaim.Name(pod, podClaim)\n   273→\t\tif err != nil {\n   274→\t\t\treturn err\n   275→\t\t}\n   276→\n   277→\t\tif claimName == nil {\n   278→\t\t\t// Nothing to do.\n   279→\t\t\tcontinue\n   280→\t\t}\n   281→\t\t// Query claim object from the API server\n   282→\t\tresourceClaim, err := m.kubeClient.ResourceV1().ResourceClaims(pod.Namespace).Get(\n   283→\t\t\tctx,\n   284→\t\t\t*claimName,\n   285→\t\t\tmetav1.GetOptions{})\n   286→\t\tif err != nil {\n   287→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"fetch ResourceClaim %s: %w\", *claimName, err)\n   288→\t\t}\n   289→\n   290→\t\tif mustCheckOwner {\n   291→\t\t\tif err = resourceclaim.IsForPod(pod, resourceClaim); err != nil {\n   292→\t\t\t\t// No wrapping, error is already informative.\n   293→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   294→\t\t\t}\n   295→\t\t}\n   296→\n   297→\t\t// Check if pod is in the ReservedFor for the claim\n   298→\t\tif !resourceclaim.IsReservedForPod(pod, resourceClaim) {\n   299→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"pod %s (%s) is not allowed to use ResourceClaim %s (%s)\",\n   300→\t\t\t\tpod.Name, pod.UID, *claimName, resourceClaim.UID)\n   301→\t\t}\n   302→\n   303→\t\t// At this point we assume that we have to prepare the claim and thus need\n   304→\t\t// the driver. If the driver is currently unavailable, it is better to fail\n   305→\t\t// even if the claim is already prepared because something is wrong with\n   306→\t\t// the node.\n   307→\t\tinfos[i].resourceClaim = resourceClaim\n   308→\t\tclaimInfo, err := newClaimInfoFromClaim(resourceClaim)\n   309→\t\tif err != nil {\n   310→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"ResourceClaim %s: %w\", resourceClaim.Name, err)\n   311→\t\t}\n   312→\t\tinfos[i].claimInfo = claimInfo\n   313→\t\tinfos[i].plugins = make(map[string]*draplugin.DRAPlugin, len(claimInfo.DriverState))\n   314→\t\tfor driverName := range claimInfo.DriverState {\n   315→\t\t\tif plugin := infos[i].plugins[driverName]; plugin != nil {\n   316→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   317→\t\t\t}\n   318→\t\t\tplugin, err := m.draPlugins.GetPlugin(driverName)\n   319→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   320→\t\t\t\t// No wrapping, error includes driver name already.\n   321→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   322→\t\t\t}\n   323→\t\t\tinfos[i].plugins[driverName] = plugin\n   324→\t\t}\n   325→\t}\n   326→\n   327→\t// Now that we have everything that we need, we can update the claim info cache.\n   328→\t// Almost nothing can go wrong anymore at this point.\n   329→\terr = m.cache.withLock(func() error {\n   330→\t\tfor i := range podResourceClaims {\n   331→\t\t\tresourceClaim := infos[i].resourceClaim\n   332→\t\t\tpodClaim := infos[i].podClaim\n   333→\t\t\tif resourceClaim == nil {\n   334→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"No need to prepare resources, no claim generated\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name)\n   335→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   336→\t\t\t}\n   337→\t\t\t// Get a reference to the claim info for this claim from the cache.\n   338→\t\t\t// If there isn't one yet, then add it to the cache.\n   339→\t\t\tclaimInfo, exists := m.cache.get(resourceClaim.Name, resourceClaim.Namespace)\n   340→\t\t\tif !exists {\n   341→\t\t\t\tclaimInfo = infos[i].claimInfo\n   342→\t\t\t\tm.cache.add(claimInfo)\n   343→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"Created new claim info cache entry\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name, \"claim\", klog.KObj(resourceClaim), \"claimInfoEntry\", claimInfo)\n   344→\t\t\t} else {\n   345→\t\t\t\tif claimInfo.ClaimUID != resourceClaim.UID {\n   346→\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"old ResourceClaim with same name %s and different UID %s still exists (previous pod force-deleted?!)\", resourceClaim.Name, claimInfo.ClaimUID)\n   347→\t\t\t\t}\n   348→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"Found existing claim info cache entry\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name, \"claim\", klog.KObj(resourceClaim), \"claimInfoEntry\", claimInfo)\n   349→\t\t\t}\n   350→\n   351→\t\t\t// Add a reference to the current pod in the claim info.\n   352→\t\t\tclaimInfo.addPodReference(pod.UID)\n   353→\n   354→\t\t\t// Checkpoint to ensure all claims we plan to prepare are tracked.\n   355→\t\t\t// If something goes wrong and the newly referenced pod gets\n   356→\t\t\t// deleted without a successful prepare call, we will catch\n   357→\t\t\t// that in the reconcile loop and take the appropriate action.\n   358→\t\t\tif err := m.cache.syncToCheckpoint(); err != nil {\n   359→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"checkpoint ResourceClaim cache: %w\", err)\n   360→\t\t\t}\n   361→\n   362→\t\t\t// If this claim is already prepared, there is no need to prepare it again.\n   363→\t\t\tif claimInfo.isPrepared() {\n   364→\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Resources already prepared\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"podClaim\", podClaim.Name, \"claim\", klog.KObj(resourceClaim))\n   365→\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   366→\t\t\t}\n   367→\n   368→\t\t\t// This saved claim will be used to update ClaimInfo cache\n   369→\t\t\t// after NodePrepareResources GRPC succeeds\n   370→\t\t\tresourceClaims[claimInfo.ClaimUID] = resourceClaim\n   371→\n   372→\t\t\t// Loop through all drivers and prepare for calling NodePrepareResources.\n   373→\t\t\tclaim := &drapb.Claim{\n   374→\t\t\t\tNamespace: claimInfo.Namespace,\n   375→\t\t\t\tUid:       string(claimInfo.ClaimUID),\n   376→\t\t\t\tName:      claimInfo.ClaimName,\n   377→\t\t\t}\n   378→\t\t\tfor driverName := range claimInfo.DriverState {\n   379→\t\t\t\tplugin := infos[i].plugins[driverName]\n   380→\t\t\t\tbatches[plugin] = append(batches[plugin], claim)\n   381→\t\t\t}\n   382→\t\t}\n   383→\n   384→\t\treturn nil\n   385→\t})\n   386→\tif err != nil {\n   387→\t\t// No error wrapping because there is no additional context needed.\n   388→\t\t// What we get here are the errors from our own callback above.\n   389→\t\treturn err\n   390→\t}\n   391→\n   392→\t// Call NodePrepareResources for all claims in each batch.\n   393→\t// If there is any error, processing gets aborted.\n   394→\t// We could try to continue, but that would make the code more complex.\n   395→\tfor plugin, claims := range batches {\n   396→\t\t// Call NodePrepareResources RPC for all resource handles.\n   397→\t\tresponse, err := plugin.NodePrepareResources(ctx, &drapb.NodePrepareResourcesRequest{Claims: claims})\n   398→\t\tif err != nil {\n   399→\t\t\t// General error unrelated to any particular claim.\n   400→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"NodePrepareResources: %w\", err)\n   401→\t\t}\n   402→\t\tfor claimUID, result := range response.Claims {\n   403→\t\t\treqClaim := lookupClaimRequest(claims, claimUID)\n   404→\t\t\tif reqClaim == nil {\n   405→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"NodePrepareResources returned result for unknown claim UID %s\", claimUID)\n   406→\t\t\t}\n   407→\t\t\tif result.GetError() != \"\" {\n   408→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"NodePrepareResources failed for ResourceClaim %s: %s\", reqClaim.Name, result.Error)\n   409→\t\t\t}\n   410→\n   411→\t\t\tclaim := resourceClaims[types.UID(claimUID)]\n   412→\n   413→\t\t\t// Add the prepared CDI devices to the claim info\n   414→\t\t\terr := m.cache.withLock(func() error {\n   415→\t\t\t\tinfo, exists := m.cache.get(claim.Name, claim.Namespace)\n   416→\t\t\t\tif !exists {\n   417→\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"internal error: unable to get claim info for ResourceClaim %s\", claim.Name)\n   418→\t\t\t\t}\n   419→\t\t\t\tfor _, device := range result.GetDevices() {\n   420→\t\t\t\t\tinfo.addDevice(plugin.DriverName(), state.Device{PoolName: device.PoolName, DeviceName: device.DeviceName, RequestNames: device.RequestNames, CDIDeviceIDs: device.CdiDeviceIds})\n   421→\t\t\t\t}\n   422→\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   423→\t\t\t})\n   424→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   425→\t\t\t\t// No wrapping, this is the error above.\n   426→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   427→\t\t\t}\n   428→\t\t}\n   429→\n   430→\t\tunfinished := len(claims) - len(response.Claims)\n   431→\t\tif unfinished != 0 {\n   432→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"NodePrepareResources skipped %d ResourceClaims\", unfinished)\n   433→\t\t}\n   434→\t}\n   435→\n   436→\t// Atomically perform some operations on the claimInfo cache.\n   437→\terr = m.cache.withLock(func() error {\n   438→\t\t// Mark all pod claims as prepared.\n   439→\t\tfor _, claim := range resourceClaims {\n   440→\t\t\tinfo, exists := m.cache.get(claim.Name, claim.Namespace)\n   441→\t\t\tif !exists {\n   442→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"internal error: unable to get claim info for ResourceClaim %s\", claim.Name)\n   443→\t\t\t}\n   444→\t\t\tinfo.setPrepared()\n   445→\t\t}\n   446→\n   447→\t\t// Checkpoint to ensure all prepared claims are tracked with their list\n   448→\t\t// of CDI devices attached.\n   449→\t\tif err := m.cache.syncToCheckpoint(); err != nil {\n   450→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"checkpoint ResourceClaim state: %w\", err)\n   451→\t\t}\n   452→\n   453→\t\treturn nil\n   454→\t})\n   455→\tif err != nil {\n   456→\t\t// No wrapping, this is the error above.\n   457→\t\treturn err\n   458→\t}\n   459→\n   460→\treturn nil\n   461→}\n   462→\n   463→func lookupClaimRequest(claims []*drapb.Claim, claimUID string) *drapb.Claim {\n   464→\tfor _, claim := range claims {\n   465→\t\tif claim.Uid == claimUID {\n   466→\t\t\treturn claim\n   467→\t\t}\n   468→\t}\n   469→\treturn nil\n   470→}\n   471→\n   472→// GetResources gets a ContainerInfo object from the claimInfo cache.\n   473→// This information is used by the caller to update a container config.\n   474→func (m *Manager) GetResources(pod *v1.Pod, container *v1.Container) (*ContainerInfo, error) {\n   475→\tcdiDevices := []kubecontainer.CDIDevice{}\n   476→\n   477→\tfor i := range pod.Spec.ResourceClaims {\n   478→\t\tpodClaim := &pod.Spec.ResourceClaims[i]\n   479→\t\tclaimName, _, err := resourceclaim.Name(pod, podClaim)\n   480→\t\tif err != nil {\n   481→\t\t\t// No wrapping, error is already informative.\n   482→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   483→\t\t}\n   484→\t\t// The claim name might be nil if no underlying resource claim\n   485→\t\t// was generated for the referenced claim. There are valid use\n   486→\t\t// cases when this might happen, so we simply skip it.\n   487→\t\tif claimName == nil {\n   488→\t\t\tcontinue\n   489→\t\t}\n   490→\t\tfor _, claim := range container.Resources.Claims {\n   491→\t\t\tif podClaim.Name != claim.Name {\n   492→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   493→\t\t\t}\n   494→\n   495→\t\t\terr := m.cache.withRLock(func() error {\n   496→\t\t\t\tclaimInfo, exists := m.cache.get(*claimName, pod.Namespace)\n   497→\t\t\t\tif !exists {\n   498→\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"internal error: unable to get claim info for ResourceClaim %s\", *claimName)\n   499→\t\t\t\t}\n   500→\n   501→\t\t\t\t// As of Kubernetes 1.31, CDI device IDs are not passed via annotations anymore.\n   502→\t\t\t\tcdiDevices = append(cdiDevices, claimInfo.cdiDevicesAsList(claim.Request)...)\n   503→\n   504→\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   505→\t\t\t})\n   506→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   507→\t\t\t\t// No wrapping, this is the error above.\n   508→\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   509→\t\t\t}\n   510→\t\t}\n   511→\t}\n   512→\n   513→\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(kubefeatures.DRAExtendedResource) && pod.Status.ExtendedResourceClaimStatus != nil {\n   514→\t\tclaimName := pod.Status.ExtendedResourceClaimStatus.ResourceClaimName\n   515→\t\t// if the container has requests for extended resources backed by DRA,\n   516→\t\t// they must have been allocated via the extendedResourceClaim created\n   517→\t\t// by the kube-scheduler.\n   518→\t\terr := m.cache.withRLock(func() error {\n   519→\t\t\tclaimInfo, exists := m.cache.get(claimName, pod.Namespace)\n   520→\t\t\tif !exists {\n   521→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unable to get claim info for claim %s in namespace %s\", claimName, pod.Namespace)\n   522→\t\t\t}\n   523→\n   524→\t\t\tfor rName, rValue := range container.Resources.Requests {\n   525→\t\t\t\tif rValue.IsZero() {\n   526→\t\t\t\t\t// We only care about the resources requested by the pod\n   527→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   528→\t\t\t\t}\n   529→\t\t\t\tif schedutil.IsDRAExtendedResourceName(rName) {\n   530→\t\t\t\t\trequestName := \"\"\n   531→\t\t\t\t\tfor _, rm := range pod.Status.ExtendedResourceClaimStatus.RequestMappings {\n   532→\t\t\t\t\t\tif rm.ContainerName == container.Name && rm.ResourceName == rName.String() {\n   533→\t\t\t\t\t\t\trequestName = rm.RequestName\n   534→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   535→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   536→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   537→\t\t\t\t\tif requestName != \"\" {\n   538→\t\t\t\t\t\t// As of Kubernetes 1.31, CDI device IDs are not passed via annotations anymore.\n   539→\t\t\t\t\t\tcdiDevices = append(cdiDevices, claimInfo.cdiDevicesAsList(requestName)...)\n   540→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   541→\t\t\t\t}\n   542→\t\t\t}\n   543→\t\t\treturn nil\n   544→\t\t})\n   545→\t\tif err != nil {\n   546→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   547→\t\t}\n   548→\t}\n   549→\treturn &ContainerInfo{CDIDevices: cdiDevices}, nil\n   550→}\n   551→\n   552→// UnprepareResources calls a driver's NodeUnprepareResource API for each resource claim owned by a pod.\n   553→// This function is idempotent and may be called multiple times against the same pod.\n   554→// As such, calls to the underlying NodeUnprepareResource API are skipped for claims that have\n   555→// already been successfully unprepared.\n   556→func (m *Manager) UnprepareResources(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod) error {\n   557→\tstartTime := time.Now()\n   558→\terr := m.unprepareResourcesForPod(ctx, pod)\n   559→\tkubeletmetrics.DRAOperationsDuration.WithLabelValues(\"UnprepareResources\", strconv.FormatBool(err == nil)).Observe(time.Since(startTime).Seconds())\n   560→\tif err != nil {\n   561→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unprepare dynamic resources: %w\", err)\n   562→\t}\n   563→\treturn nil\n   564→}\n   565→\n   566→func (m *Manager) unprepareResourcesForPod(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod) error {\n   567→\tvar claimNames []string\n   568→\tfor i := range pod.Spec.ResourceClaims {\n   569→\t\tclaimName, _, err := resourceclaim.Name(pod, &pod.Spec.ResourceClaims[i])\n   570→\t\tif err != nil {\n   571→\t\t\t// No wrapping, the error is already informative.\n   572→\t\t\treturn err\n   573→\t\t}\n   574→\t\t// The claim name might be nil if no underlying resource claim\n   575→\t\t// was generated for the referenced claim. There are valid use\n   576→\t\t// cases when this might happen, so we simply skip it.\n   577→\t\tif claimName == nil {\n   578→\t\t\tcontinue\n   579→\t\t}\n   580→\t\tclaimNames = append(claimNames, *claimName)\n   581→\t}\n   582→\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(kubefeatures.DRAExtendedResource) {\n   583→\t\tif pod.Status.ExtendedResourceClaimStatus != nil {\n   584→\t\t\tclaimNames = append(claimNames, pod.Status.ExtendedResourceClaimStatus.ResourceClaimName)\n   585→\t\t}\n   586→\t}\n   587→\n   588→\treturn m.unprepareResources(ctx, pod.UID, pod.Namespace, claimNames)\n   589→}\n   590→\n   591→func (m *Manager) unprepareResources(ctx context.Context, podUID types.UID, namespace string, claimNames []string) error {\n   592→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   593→\tbatches := make(map[string][]*drapb.Claim)\n   594→\tclaimNamesMap := make(map[types.UID]string)\n   595→\tfor _, claimName := range claimNames {\n   596→\t\t// Atomically perform some operations on the claimInfo cache.\n   597→\t\terr := m.cache.withLock(func() error {\n   598→\t\t\t// Get the claim info from the cache\n   599→\t\t\tclaimInfo, exists := m.cache.get(claimName, namespace)\n   600→\n   601→\t\t\t// Skip calling NodeUnprepareResource if claim info is not cached\n   602→\t\t\tif !exists {\n   603→\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   604→\t\t\t}\n   605→\n   606→\t\t\t// Skip calling NodeUnprepareResource if other pods are still referencing it\n   607→\t\t\tif len(claimInfo.PodUIDs) > 1 {\n   608→\t\t\t\t// We delay checkpointing of this change until\n   609→\t\t\t\t// UnprepareResources returns successfully. It is OK to do\n   610→\t\t\t\t// this because we will only return successfully from this call\n   611→\t\t\t\t// if the checkpoint has succeeded. That means if the kubelet\n   612→\t\t\t\t// is ever restarted before this checkpoint succeeds, we will\n   613→\t\t\t\t// simply call into this (idempotent) function again.\n   614→\t\t\t\tclaimInfo.deletePodReference(podUID)\n   615→\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   616→\t\t\t}\n   617→\n   618→\t\t\t// This claimInfo name will be used to update ClaimInfo cache\n   619→\t\t\t// after NodeUnprepareResources GRPC succeeds\n   620→\t\t\tclaimNamesMap[claimInfo.ClaimUID] = claimInfo.ClaimName\n   621→\n   622→\t\t\t// Loop through all drivers and prepare for calling NodeUnprepareResources.\n   623→\t\t\tclaim := &drapb.Claim{\n   624→\t\t\t\tNamespace: claimInfo.Namespace,\n   625→\t\t\t\tUid:       string(claimInfo.ClaimUID),\n   626→\t\t\t\tName:      claimInfo.ClaimName,\n   627→\t\t\t}\n   628→\t\t\tfor driverName := range claimInfo.DriverState {\n   629→\t\t\t\tbatches[driverName] = append(batches[driverName], claim)\n   630→\t\t\t}\n   631→\n   632→\t\t\treturn nil\n   633→\t\t})\n   634→\t\tif err != nil {\n   635→\t\t\t// No wrapping, this is the error above.\n   636→\t\t\treturn err\n   637→\t\t}\n   638→\t}\n   639→\n   640→\t// Call NodeUnprepareResources for all claims in each batch.\n   641→\t// If there is any error, processing gets aborted.\n   642→\t// We could try to continue, but that would make the code more complex.\n   643→\tfor driverName, claims := range batches {\n   644→\t\t// Call NodeUnprepareResources RPC for all resource handles.\n   645→\t\tplugin, err := m.draPlugins.GetPlugin(driverName)\n   646→\t\tif plugin == nil {\n   647→\t\t\t// No wrapping, error includes driver name already.\n   648→\t\t\treturn err\n   649→\t\t}\n   650→\t\tresponse, err := plugin.NodeUnprepareResources(ctx, &drapb.NodeUnprepareResourcesRequest{Claims: claims})\n   651→\t\tif err != nil {\n   652→\t\t\t// General error unrelated to any particular claim.\n   653→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"NodeUnprepareResources: %w\", err)\n   654→\t\t}\n   655→\n   656→\t\tfor claimUID, result := range response.Claims {\n   657→\t\t\treqClaim := lookupClaimRequest(claims, claimUID)\n   658→\t\t\tif reqClaim == nil {\n   659→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"NodeUnprepareResources returned result for unknown claim UID %s\", claimUID)\n   660→\t\t\t}\n   661→\t\t\tif result.GetError() != \"\" {\n   662→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"NodeUnprepareResources failed for ResourceClaim %s: %s\", reqClaim.Name, result.Error)\n   663→\t\t\t}\n   664→\t\t}\n   665→\n   666→\t\tunfinished := len(claims) - len(response.Claims)\n   667→\t\tif unfinished != 0 {\n   668→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"NodeUnprepareResources skipped %d ResourceClaims\", unfinished)\n   669→\t\t}\n   670→\t}\n   671→\n   672→\t// Atomically perform some operations on the claimInfo cache.\n   673→\terr := m.cache.withLock(func() error {\n   674→\t\t// TODO(#132978): Re-evaluate this logic to support post-mortem health updates.\n   675→\t\t// As of the initial implementation, we immediately delete the claim info upon\n   676→\t\t// unprepare. This means a late-arriving health update for a terminated pod\n   677→\t\t// will be missed. A future enhancement could be to \"tombstone\" this entry for\n   678→\t\t// a grace period instead of deleting it.\n   679→\n   680→\t\t// Delete all claimInfos from the cache that have just been unprepared.\n   681→\t\tfor _, claimName := range claimNamesMap {\n   682→\t\t\tclaimInfo, _ := m.cache.get(claimName, namespace)\n   683→\t\t\tm.cache.delete(claimName, namespace)\n   684→\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"Deleted claim info cache entry\", \"claim\", klog.KRef(namespace, claimName), \"claimInfoEntry\", claimInfo)\n   685→\t\t}\n   686→\n   687→\t\t// Atomically sync the cache back to the checkpoint.\n   688→\t\tif err := m.cache.syncToCheckpoint(); err != nil {\n   689→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"checkpoint ResourceClaim state: %w\", err)\n   690→\t\t}\n   691→\t\treturn nil\n   692→\t})\n   693→\tif err != nil {\n   694→\t\t// No wrapping, this is the error above.\n   695→\t\treturn err\n   696→\t}\n   697→\n   698→\treturn nil\n   699→}\n   700→\n   701→// PodMightNeedToUnprepareResources returns true if the pod might need to\n   702→// unprepare resources\n   703→func (m *Manager) PodMightNeedToUnprepareResources(uid types.UID) bool {\n   704→\tm.cache.Lock()\n   705→\tdefer m.cache.Unlock()\n   706→\treturn m.cache.hasPodReference(uid)\n   707→}\n   708→\n   709→// GetContainerClaimInfos gets Container's ClaimInfo\n   710→func (m Currently, `AllocationMode: All` is technically unrestricted by code enforcement, but is implicitly single-node due to device pool constraints. The change would enable cluster-wide device enumeration and allocation, affecting scheduler hot paths (Filter phase), kubelet device preparation, controller reallocation logic, and resource exhaustion handling across all DRA components.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe DRA allocation system uses three key control mechanisms:\n1. **AllocationMode** (ExactCount vs All) - Controls allocation quantity semantics\n2. **BindsToNode** - Controls whether allocation is tied to a single node\n3. **NodeSelector/DeviceNodeSelection** - Controls which nodes can use allocated devices\n\nThe current architecture assumes `AllocationMode: All` operates within pool boundaries that naturally restrict to single nodes. The proposed change would decouple AllocationMode from implicit node restrictions, creating scenarios where a single claim requests ALL devices across multiple nodes. Currently, `AllocationMode: All` is technically unrestricted by code enforcement, but is implicitly single-node due to device pool constraints. The change would enable cluster-wide device enumeration and allocation, affecting scheduler hot paths (Filter phase), kubelet device preparation, controller reallocation logic, and resource exhaustion handling across all DRA components.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe DRA allocation system uses three key control mechanisms:\n1. **AllocationMode** (ExactCount vs All) - Controls allocation quantity semantics\n2. **BindsToNode** - Controls whether allocation is tied to a single node\n3. **NodeSelector/DeviceNodeSelection** - Controls which nodes can use allocated devices\n\nThe current architecture assumes `AllocationMode: All` operates within pool boundaries that naturally restrict to single nodes. The proposed change would decouple AllocationMode from implicit node restrictions, creating scenarios where a single claim requests ALL devices across multiple nodes. This impacts:\n- Scheduler's Filter phase (must evaluate and allocate devices across cluster)\n- Kubelet's device preparation on multiple nodes\n- Controller's reservation and deallocation logic\n- Performance characteristics of allocator loops\n\n## Evidence\n\n### 1.
